    I.

    acintyo niṣkalaḥ śāntaḥ,

    dhruva-m abyaya-m īśvaraḥ,

    asau sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śāntaḥ,

    śivaḥ sakalaniṣkalaḥ ◆

    II.

    cittavṛttinirodhākhyaḥ,

    yogaḥ paramadurlabhaḥ,

    tasmin yoge samārabdhe,

    svayam ātmā prakāśate


    kaṅ katutur i cittavṛtti, ya sinaṅguh yoga ṅara⟨ms: 55r⟩nya, ndān atyanta ivәhnyān⟨lb⟩ inabhyāsa, apan tan harәp jātiniṅ vaṅ riṅ gave makas, kunaṅ saṅ vairāgya,⟨lb⟩ saṅ huvus varәg ri lārani janma, sira mahyun ri yoga, apan maharәp ri suka viśeṣa⟨lb⟩ ṅaranya ⟨,⟩ ikaṅ paṅguhan i jāti saṅ hyaṅ ātmā ya sinaṅguh suka viśeṣa⟨lb⟩ ṅaranya, yan apa yan kapaṅguh jāti saṅ hyaṅ ātmā, yan ginavayakәn ikaṅ⟨lb⟩ yogātah,

    sumahur saṅ kumāra,

    tan kagavaya ikaṅ yoga kahiḍәp tah saṅ hyaṅ ātmā de mami,⟨lb⟩ tamatan ātmā ikā liṅta, yekiṅ citta ṅaranya, mataṅnyan sinaṅguh citta, apan⟨lb⟩ ekaviṣayanya, ya mataṅnya⟨ms: 55v⟩n citta juga kahiḍәp denya, sumahur saṅ pāra,⟨lb⟩ ndya vṛttinya, mataṅnyan citta ṅaranya, nihan grahaṇa, viparyaya, vikalpa,⟨lb⟩ nidrā, smṛti,

    tәlas sinurat iṅ antiraga pun, iti dharma pātañjala samāpta ◆ titi māsa padūpvan vulan kasapuluh, pañcavara, u, trivara, dva, saptavara, a, aṣṭavara, yama, vuku vuyai, i śaka, parab iṅ sakala lavaṅ gajah guṇa vvaṅ ◆

    Bibliography

    Andrea Acri edited this text over the years 2006–2011, and published the first editions of it in 2011, the second in 2017. He typed and maintained a text file (2006–2018) which was cast into a TEI structure over the years Converted the text to TEI format 2018–2023. The transcription was changed to comply with DHARMA norms in 2023.

    In this digital edition, corrections of misprints in the 2011 edition, as well as more substantial changes (e.g, alternative emendations/reconstructions), have been applied on the basis of the 2017 edition; corrections of misprints in the 2017 edition have been applied tacitly.

    Acri, Andrea. 2011. Dharma Pātañjala: a Śaiva scripture from ancient Java studied in the light of related old Javanese and Sanskrit texts. Groningen: Forsten.

    Acri, Andrea. 2017. Dharma Pātañjala: A Śaiva scripture from ancient Java, studied in the light or related old Javanese and Sanskrit texts. Second Edition. New Delhi: International Academy of Indian Culture and Aditya Prakashan.

    . <p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.132">aku huvus maṅhiḍәp saṅsāra, aneka ikaṅ janma bhinuktiku<supplied reason="omitted">,</supplied> vәkasan<surplus>,</surplus><lb/>
    720tәkani ga<pb n="46v" edRef="ms"/>veṅku hayu, kavava tāku ri saṅ paṇḍita, vinarah tāku riṅ dhar<lb break="no"/>maśāstra, ya ta inabhyāsaṅku, alavas pvāku gumavayakәn ikaṅ dharmaśās<lb break="no"/>tra, mati tāku, <surplus>muvah taku,</surplus> muvah tāku maṅjanma mānuṣa, atutur tāku ri<lb/>
    .janmaṅku, muvah tāku humulunakәn śarīraṅku ri saṅ paṇḍita, vinarah tāku<lb/>

    .ikā, ya ta mataṅnyan paṅhulihuliha ri hati, aku ahāta tutakneṅkva pasyaṅ<lb break="no"/>nikaṅ devatā byaktāku mahiḍәp saṅsāra muvah, apan jātiniṅ śaktiniṅ vi<lb break="no"/>ṣaya, luput ikaṅ suka viśeṣa denya, ikaṅ lāra tan vuruṅ kabhukti deku, ikaṅ<lb/>
    .kasiddhyan huvus kabhukti deku, tan ulihkv aṅinakinak, hulihkv agave brata<lb/>
    1225lāvan samādhi, sajīvaniṅ rāt ikā, hilaṅa pva ya deniṅ viṣaya sakarәṅ, lalu kaś<lb break="no"/>malaṅku, pakṣani kahanan ikā, indrajālasādṛ<pb n="84r" edRef="ms"/>śya, kadi kilat kabhuktinya,<lb/>
    .yadyan malavas i bhinukti, ndātan vuruṅ maveh lāra, ikaṅ lāra, aneka lvir<lb break="no"/>nya, yāvat pvekaṅ janma katibān lāra, tāvat <sic>kadasyatanayā</sic>, mevәh maluy<lb/>
    .janma muvah, aṅhiṅ kәbho sapi asu vәk tәmahanya, yekā katakutku kamu<lb/>
    .manah, yan aṅgānәn pasyaṅnikaṅ vatәk devatā, maṅkana liṅnira varah<lb break="no"/>varah ry avaknira,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.258">nihan sahur saṅ para, satus kvehanikaṅ viṣaya kabhukti deniṅ vvaṅ,<lb/>
    1230 tan ya maṅhiḍәpa lāra yan vruh ri katattvan bhaṭāra, mataṅnyan maṅkana, <lb/>
    . apan tan hana tu<pb n="84v" edRef="ms"/>hutuhun ikaṅ ulah kabeh, mataṅnyan tan hana tuhu, an<lb/>
    . hilaṅa donikā kabeh, maluya ri saṅkanya, ndi saṅkanya, saṅke saṅ hyaṅ<lb/>
    . tayā, malilaṅ tan kāvaraṇan, sira sinaṅguh <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">niṣkala</foreign> ṅaranya, anuṅ kalīnaniṅ <lb/>
    .rāt kabeh, niyata tan salah paran, maṅkana pva katattvaniṅ janma, mvaṅ <lb/>
    1235kavruhan saṅ hyaṅ paramārtha,</p>
    .
    . <pb n="334"/>
    .
    .
    1240<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.259">ndya ta mataṅnyan saṅśaya riṅ ulah kabeh, apa mataṅnyan pamuhāra lāra,<lb/>
    . kabhuktyaniṅ viṣaya, maṅkana ta kәbho sapi asu vәk, sabarinyān mati mulih<lb/>
    . ri tayā, tamatan dinalih mulih riṅ tayā, apan katon hilaṅ <pb n="85r" edRef="ms"/> ikaṅ avaknya, yekā<lb/>
    .inakunta mokṣa, jñānanya lāvan cittanya tan avruh irikā, lāvan ikaṅ tayā<lb/>
    .an sinaṅguh paramārtha, apa ta paṅupakāranya, ndya kasiddhyan kadadi<lb/>
    1245 denya, sumahur saṅ para, tan <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">mokṣa</foreign> ta ṅaran ikā, yan pamaṅguha kasid<lb break="no"/>dhyan, kunaṅ yan hilaṅ juga, ya <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">mokṣa</foreign> ṅaranya, yan kva liṅa saṅ para, ka<lb break="no"/>pan ta kәta yan tәka, apan dudū ikaṅ ahurip, kadi laṅgə̄ṅnikaṅ hana, kapan tekaṅ tayā yan ta pratyakṣa, sumahur saṅ para, dlāha ri tәkani pralaya, yan<lb/>
    .tayā ikaṅ rāt kabeh, maṅkana liṅ saṅ para, <pb n="85v" edRef="ms"/> apa yan mәtu ikā rat kabeh mu<lb break="no"/>vah, yekā mājarakәn yan līna ri tayā ikaṅ rāt, apan saṅkeṅ tayā saṅkanya<lb/>
    .mәtu ṅūni, yan maṅkana liṅa saṅ para, viruddha tekā pakṣanta yan maṅ<lb break="no"/>kana, mataṅnyan sinaṅguh viruddha, apan līna riṅ tayā ikaṅ jagat liṅta,<lb/>
    .mәtu pva ya mәne sinaṅguh ta mәtu saṅkeṅ tayā ikaṅ jagat, adva tan tayā<lb/>
    .ṅaranikā, yan kalīnani jagat an vәtu, yan kva liṅa saṅ para, tan dadi taṅ <lb/>
    1250paramārtha maṅkana,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.260">sumahur saṅ kumāra,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.261"><!--<label type="question" n="38"/>--> aparan ikaṅ sinaṅguh saṅ para tayā ulihaniṅ jagat, lāvan saṅkaniṅ jagat <lb/>
    . mәtu, kasiha<pb n="86r" edRef="ms"/>na varahәn ṅhulun bhaṭāra, <lb/>
    . ikaṅ sinaṅguh saṅ para tayā paramārtha, yekāna sinaṅguh <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">prakṛtilīna</foreign>, tayā <lb/>
    1255pasaṅganiṅ citta sattva rajah tamah, lakṣaṇanya pәtaṅ tan pacetanā, apan <lb/>
    .tan hana kaprajñān iriya,</p>
    .
    . <pb n="336"/>
    .
    1260<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.262">ṅuniveh ikaṅ cetanā, apa mataṅnyan sinaṅguh ulihaniṅ jagat apan ya ikā<lb/>
    . <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">kriyāśakti bhaṭāra</foreign> ṅaranya, māyāmāyā ikā ātmā<supplied reason="omitted">,</supplied> ya ta khyāti bhaṭāra para<lb break="no"/>makāraṇa, yāvat pvekaṅ ātmā cumetanekaṅ prakṛtitattva, tāvat mәtu ikaṅ<lb/>
    .jagat, yapvan mari ikaṅ prakṛtitattva ci<pb n="86v" edRef="ms"/>netanā deniraṅ ātmā, līna ikaṅ jagat <lb/>
    .maluy ri saṅkanya ri prakṛtitattva, maṅkana sthitinikaṅ rāt saṅkanya ṅūni,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.263">sumahur saṅ kumāra,</p>
    1265<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.264"><!--<label type="question" n="39"/>--> apa dumehnikaṅ prakṛtitattva sәṅguhәn tayā de saṅ para,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.265">sumahur bhaṭāra,</p>
    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.266">apan tan hiḍәpnya, ṅuniveh ikaṅ lakṣaṇa, tan paramārtha pvekaṅ tayā sin<lb break="no"/>aṅguh saṅ para <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">viśeṣa</foreign>, taha tan paramārtha ikā, apan saṅkani jagat lāvan<lb/>
    .ulihanya, mvaṅ inulihakәn taya, vruh pva saṅ yogi, an tan paramārtha ikaṅ<lb/>
    .tayā, ya ta mataṅnyan tan ikā phalani <pb n="87r" edRef="ms"/> samādhi saṅ yogi, ndya ta lakṣaṇa<lb/>
    1270saṅ hyaṅ paramārtha, anuṅ tujuni samādhi saṅ yogi, yan kva liṅanta, ikaṅ<lb/>
    .cetanā sarvajña saṅ kumavruhi ikaṅ rāt kabeh, sarvakāryakartā, saṅ gumave<lb/>
    .ikaṅ rāt kabeh, ndi ta kahananira, yan kva liṅanta, kahananira ikaṅ rāt kabeh,<lb/>
    .ndātan katon, apan tan palakṣaṇa, tan parūpa, tan pahiḍәp, pisaniṅu, apa<lb/>
    .byaktanyān hana, yan kva liṅanta, nihan utpattisthitilīnani jagat, yeka ic<lb break="no"/>chā bhaṭāra, ikaṅ prakṛtitattva, ya sinaṅguh <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">niṣkala</foreign> ṅaranya, a<pb n="87v" edRef="ms"/>hyun pva sira<lb/>
    1275gumavaya jagat ya mataṅnyan taṅ ātmā cumetanekaṅ prakṛtitattva, mataṅ<lb break="no"/>nyan mәtu nāda saṅkeṅ niṣkala, saṅke nāda mәtu taṅ vindu, saṅkeṅ vindu<lb/>
    .mәtu taṅ ardhacandra, saṅke ardhacandra, mәtu ta oṁkāra, saṅkeṅ oṁkāra<lb/>
    . mәtu taṅ tryakṣara, <supplied reason="omitted">saṅkeṅ tryakṣara</supplied> mәtu taṅ pañcākṣara, saṅkeṅ pañ<lb break="no"/>cākṣara, mәtu taṅ jagat kabeh, nāhan lakṣaṇanikaṅ niṣkalatattvān pamәt<lb break="no"/>vakәna jagat,</p>

    .<p xml:id="dharmaPatanjala_01.267">sumahur saṅ para, kadi saṅkeṅ prakṛti ikaṅ vindu nāda, apan saṅkeṅ bhaṭāra<lb/>
    . ikaṅ vindu nāda mәtu, yan maṅkana liṅa saṅ para, yan dadya taṅ dharma<lb/>
    . tuṅgal sumaṇḍaṅa dha<pb n="88r" edRef="ms"/>rma rva, ndya dharma rva ṅaranya, nyaṅ cetanā lā<lb break="no"/>van acetanā, <supplied reason="lost">n</supplied>dya ṅaranya cetanā, bhaṭāra paramakāraṇa, ndya acetanā<lb/>
    1285ṅaranya, nyaṅ prakṛtitattva, yekā tan dadi pinakadharmān atuṅgal, padanya,<lb/>
    .kadyaṅgāniṅ tәṅah ṅve, sәṅguhәn ta tәṅah vәṅi, apa mataṅnyan tan dadi<lb/>
    .maṅkana bhaṭāra, apan sira vәnaṅ makecchā ikaṅ rat kabeh, yan maṅkana<lb/>
    .liṅa saṅ para, saṅsāra kapva bhaṭāra yan maṅkana, sadenyan saṅsāra bha<lb break="no"/>ṭāra, yan kva liṅa saṅ para, tan palvir kapva ikiṅ rāt kabeh, denyan tan palvir<lb/>
    .ike jagat, apa yan kasaṅśayakna, yan maṅ<pb n="88v" edRef="ms"/>kana liṅa saṅ para, ndya jagat tan<lb/>
    1290palvir tinonta, apan ta pva pratyakṣa ya, yāvat tan palvir ikaṅ jagat, tāvat<lb/>
    . <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">pralaya</foreign>, <foreign xml:lang="san-Latn">pralaya</foreign> ṅaranya, mәtu vaḍavānala yan tәkā, apan icchā bhaṭāra in<lb break="no"/>apekṣānya, ◉</p>
